        function parseLine(line){
            return "<" + line[0] +" data-cont='"+ line[1] +"'></" + line[0] + ">";
        }
        function proccessHTMLArray(obj){
            if(typeof(obj[0]) == 'string' && typeof(obj[1]) == 'string'){
                return "<" + obj[0] +" data-cont='"+ obj[1] +"'></" + obj[0] + ">";
            }else if(typeof(obj[0]) == 'string' && typeof(obj[1]) == 'object' && typeof(obj[1][0]) == 'string'){
                var attr = "";
                if(obj[0] == "a"){
                    attr = " href='"+ obj[2]+"'";
                }
                return "<" + obj[0] + attr + ">"+ proccessHTMLArray(obj[1]) +"</" + obj[0] + ">";
            }else if(typeof(obj[0]) == 'string' && typeof(obj[1]) == 'object' && typeof(obj[1][0]) == 'object'){
                var loopValues = "";
                loopValues += "<" + obj[0] + ">"; 
                for(var subObjs = 0; subObjs < obj[1].length; subObjs++){
                    loopValues += proccessHTMLArray(obj[1][subObjs]);
                }
                loopValues += "</" + obj[0] + ">"; 
                return loopValues;
            }
        }
`

        function parseLine(line){
            return "<" + line[0] +" data-cont='"+ line[1] +"'></" + line[0] + ">";
        }
        function proccessHTMLArray(obj){
            if(typeof(obj[0]) == 'string' && typeof(obj[1]) == 'string'){
                return "<" + obj[0] +" data-cont='"+ obj[1] +"'></" + obj[0] + ">";
            }else if(typeof(obj[0]) == 'string' && typeof(obj[1]) == 'object' && typeof(obj[1][0]) == 'string'){
                var attr = "";
                if(obj[0] == "a"){
                    attr = " href='"+ obj[2]+"'";
                }
                return "<" + obj[0] + attr + ">"+ proccessHTMLArray(obj[1]) +"</" + obj[0] + ">";
            }else if(typeof(obj[0]) == 'string' && typeof(obj[1]) == 'object' && typeof(obj[1][0]) == 'object'){
                var loopValues = "";
                loopValues += "<" + obj[0] + ">"; 
                for(var subObjs = 0; subObjs < obj[1].length; subObjs++){
                    loopValues += proccessHTMLArray(obj[1][subObjs]);
                }
                loopValues += "</" + obj[0] + ">"; 
                return loopValues;
            }
        }
